NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
T. John Kennady alias John Kenedy, a male child born to Thomas on 11th August 1981, residing at No. 11,
Aravanigal Street, New Nagar, Ayyan Koilpattu, Ayyur Agaram Post, Villupuram-605 602, has been living as a Female after
sexual reassignment Surgery by Dr. S.A.K. Meeran, M.S. (Gen), Senior Surgical Consultant, Madurai Surgical Hospital,
Dindigul, (Reg.No.17952). By this I may be treated as a Female and shall henceforth be known as T. RUBINI.
Villupuram,
20th March 2015.

T. JOHN KENNADY alias JOHN KENEDY.

A. Sivasankar, a male child born to A. Appasamy on 16th December 1974, residing at No. 1, P-Block, 69-A Street,
Jafferkhanpet, Chennai-600 083, has been living as Female after an elaborate sexual reassignment surgery by
Dr. Dhanasekaran, M.S. Ortho, D. Ortho, Reg.No.64905, Asst. Surgeon, Government Peripheral Hospital, K.K. Nagar,
by this I may be treated as a Female and shall henceforth be known as A. SIVASANKARI.
Chennai,
20th March 2015.

A. SIVASANKAR.
